< Review>
This bus station is a front & has no attendants or security. You cannot go inside as it is a locked abandoned building. If you are looking to catch the Greyhound or Amtrak connection bus, you will be forced to stand on the side of the street while you wait for it to arrive. Your only other option would be to stop by the Chico Art Center and be kicked out by the owners, a building which is right next door to this excuse for a bus station. While I was visiting Chico State for a campus tour, I had to come here to catch the bus and was harassed by a homeless man. Im only 19 and live 7 hours away from Chico. The Chico Art Center staff specifically the owner refused to help shelter me, so I was forced to sit outside alone while my bus was still 2 hours away. Come here if you want to risk your life with no chance of help from anyone who lives here.</Review>

<user>106735407793597887921</user><username>Max< /username>< Date>
1579560021700< /Date>
< rate>
1</rate>
< Review>
While the Greyhound bus is a cheap way to get to where I'm going, it's so often unreliable that I've come to expect major problems whenever I use their bus. The bus is often very late, if it even shows up at all. Sometimes it shows up on time or without too long a wait, but in my experience, it's about 50/50, which isn't very reliable for a bus service, especially if I need to get to the airport to catch a flight on time. I've waited for hours and hours, unsure of whether the bus was ever going to show, and unsure of how I'd get to my destination on time and whether to keep waiting, or find another method of transportation. Refunding your ticket is difficult, you need to send your ticket in by postal service mail to be considered. My last ticket was an e-ticket, so I submitted a request twice on their website asking how to refund an e-ticket and haven't gotten a response yet. The buses aren't too clean, I often find trash left behind by other riders, and the back of the bus smells due to the bathroom (which is nice to have for long bus rides, but I wish it was kept cleaner). This particular station (Chico) is often closed, so it's more like a bus stop.<//Review>

<rating>5</rating>< review>
My husband and I found a dog running on North River road this morning. We were able to catch him and brought him into animal regulations. The staff were extremely grateful to us for rescuing him and they immediately took him into their care. He did not appear to have any injuries but they checked him thoroughly. It was very hard to avoid the temptation to adopt him on the spot but the staff were so caring they made me feel that he was in good hands.
We have adopted 5 dogs from this facility, 2 of which are still with us. This facility does an AMAZING job and we would adopt more if we could. And we will not adopt from anywhere else.< /review>
